diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/FileWatcher.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/FileWatcher.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..34c6d74
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/FileWatcher.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,103 @@
+import Foundation
+
+final class FileWatcher: @unchecked Sendable {
+    enum Event {
+        case modified
+        case deleted
+    }
+
+    private let url: URL
+    private let callback: (Event) -> Void
+    private var source: DispatchSourceFileSystemObject?
+    private var fileDescriptor: Int32 = -1
+    private let retryDelay: TimeInterval = 0.1
+    private let maxRetries: Int = 3
+
+    init(url: URL, callback: @escaping (Event) -> Void) {
+        self.url = url
+        self.callback = callback
+    }
+
+    func start() {
+        fileDescriptor = open(url.path, O_EVTONLY)
+        guard fileDescriptor >= 0 else {
+            callback(.deleted)
+            return
+        }
+
+        let source = DispatchSource.makeFileSystemObjectSource(
+            fileDescriptor: fileDescriptor,
+            eventMask: [.write, .delete, .rename],
+            queue: .global(qos: .utility)
+        )
+
+        source.setEventHandler { [weak self] in
+            guard let self else { return }
+            let flags = source.data
+            if flags.contains(.delete) || flags.contains(.rename) {
+                self.handleDeleteOrRename()
+            } else if flags.contains(.write) {
+                self.handleWrite()
+            }
+        }
+
+        // No cancel handler that closes fd — we close fd synchronously in stop()
+        // to avoid race conditions when stop() + start() are called in sequence.
+
+        source.resume()
+        self.source = source
+    }
+
+    func stop() {
+        source?.cancel()
+        source = nil
+        if fileDescriptor >= 0 {
+            close(fileDescriptor)
+            fileDescriptor = -1
+        }
+    }
+
+    private func handleWrite() {
+        readWithRetry(attempt: 0)
+    }
+
+    private func readWithRetry(attempt: Int) {
+        if FileManager.default.isReadableFile(atPath: url.path) {
+            callback(.modified)
+        } else if attempt < maxRetries {
+            DispatchQueue.global().asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + retryDelay) {
+                self.readWithRetry(attempt: attempt + 1)
+            }
+        } else {
+            callback(.deleted)
+        }
+    }
+
+    private func handleDeleteOrRename() {
+        // Editors often save by renaming the file away and recreating it.
+        // Wait briefly then re-check existence. Use multiple retries for
+        // slower save operations.
+        retryRestart(attempt: 0, maxAttempts: 5, delay: 0.2)
+    }
+
+    private func retryRestart(attempt: Int, maxAttempts: Int, delay: TimeInterval) {
+        DispatchQueue.global().asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + delay) { [weak self] in
+            guard let self else { return }
+            if FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: self.url.path) {
+                // File was re-created — restart monitoring
+                self.stop()
+                self.start()
+                self.callback(.modified)
+            } else if attempt < maxAttempts {
+                // File not yet recreated — retry with increasing delay
+                self.retryRestart(attempt: attempt + 1, maxAttempts: maxAttempts, delay: delay)
+            } else {
+                self.callback(.deleted)
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    deinit {
+        stop()
+    }
+}
diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/HTMLTemplate.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/HTMLTemplate.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..dcf39e5
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/HTMLTemplate.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,97 @@
+import Foundation
+
+enum HTMLTemplate {
+    static func build(
+        markdownContent: String,
+        markedJS: String,
+        highlightJS: String,
+        css: String
+    ) -> String {
+        let escapedMarkdown = markdownContent
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "\\", with: "\\\\")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "`", with: "\\`")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "$", with: "\\$")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "</script>", with: "<\\/script>")
+
+        return """
+        <!DOCTYPE html>
+        <html>
+        <head>
+            <meta charset="utf-8">
+            <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
+            <meta http-equiv="Content-Security-Policy" content="default-src 'none'; style-src 'unsafe-inline'; script-src 'unsafe-inline'; img-src file: data: https: http:;">
+            <style>\(css)</style>
+            <script>\(markedJS)</script>
+            <script>\(highlightJS)</script>
+        </head>
+        <body>
+            <div id="content"></div>
+            <script>
+                // Strip raw HTML blocks from markdown output for security.
+                // This prevents injected <img onerror=...>, <script>, javascript: links, etc.
+                marked.use({
+                    renderer: {
+                        html(token) { return ''; }
+                    }
+                });
+
+                // marked.js configuration: GFM enabled
+                marked.setOptions({
+                    gfm: true,
+                    breaks: false,
+                    highlight: function(code, lang) {
+                        if (lang && hljs.getLanguage(lang)) {
+                            return hljs.highlight(code, { language: lang }).value;
+                        }
+                        return code;
+                    }
+                });
+
+                // Initial render
+                const md = `\(escapedMarkdown)`;
+                document.getElementById('content').innerHTML = marked.parse(md);
+                hljs.highlightAll();
+
+                // Intercept external link clicks
+                document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+                    const link = e.target.closest('a');
+                    if (link && link.href) {
+                        const url = new URL(link.href);
+                        if (url.protocol === 'javascript:') {
+                            e.preventDefault();
+                            return;
+                        }
+                        if (url.protocol === 'http:' || url.protocol === 'https:') {
+                            e.preventDefault();
+                            window.webkit.messageHandlers.linkClicked.postMessage(link.href);
+                        }
+                    }
+                });
+
+                // Dark mode detection
+                const mediaQuery = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+                function updateTheme(e) {
+                    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme',
+                        e.matches ? 'dark' : 'light');
+                }
+                mediaQuery.addEventListener('change', updateTheme);
+                updateTheme(mediaQuery);
+
+                // Scroll position reporting
+                function reportScroll() {
+                    window.webkit.messageHandlers.scrollPosition.postMessage(window.scrollY);
+                }
+
+                // Global updateContent function for live reload
+                function updateContent(md) {
+                    const scrollY = window.scrollY;
+                    document.getElementById('content').innerHTML = marked.parse(md);
+                    hljs.highlightAll();
+                    window.scrollTo(0, Math.min(scrollY, document.body.scrollHeight));
+                }
+            </script>
+        </body>
+        </html>
+        """
+    }
+}
diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/WindowManager.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/WindowManager.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..b1adbd4
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/WindowManager.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,63 @@
+import SwiftUI
+import UniformTypeIdentifiers
+
+@MainActor
+class WindowManager: ObservableObject {
+    /// Currently open file URLs (for duplicate detection).
+    @Published private(set) var openFiles: Set<URL> = []
+
+    /// Stored reference to the openWindow action, set by the App entry point
+    /// via `OpenWindowInjector` before any file can be opened.
+    var openWindowAction: OpenWindowAction?
+
+    /// Test-only hook: called instead of `openWindowAction` when set.
+    /// Allows unit tests to exercise openFile() without a real SwiftUI environment.
+    var _testOpenWindowHandler: ((URL) -> Void)?
+
+    func openFile(_ url: URL) {
+        let resolved = url.standardizedFileURL
+        if openFiles.contains(resolved) {
+            bringToFront(resolved)
+            return
+        }
+
+        // In tests, use the test handler; in production, use the real action.
+        if let testHandler = _testOpenWindowHandler {
+            testHandler(resolved)
+        } else {
+            guard let action = openWindowAction else { return }
+            action(value: resolved)
+        }
+        openFiles.insert(resolved)
+    }
+
+    func closeFile(_ url: URL) {
+        openFiles.remove(url.standardizedFileURL)
+    }
+
+    func showOpenPanel() {
+        let panel = NSOpenPanel()
+        panel.allowedContentTypes = [
+            UTType(filenameExtension: "md")!,
+            UTType(filenameExtension: "markdown")!,
+        ]
+        panel.allowsMultipleSelection = true
+        panel.canChooseDirectories = false
+        if panel.runModal() == .OK {
+            for url in panel.urls {
+                openFile(url)
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    private func bringToFront(_ url: URL) {
+        for window in NSApp.windows {
+            // Match by representedURL (full file URL) for accurate identification
+            // when multiple files share the same basename.
+            if window.representedURL == url {
+                window.makeKeyAndOrderFront(nil)
+                return
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}
diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/ViewModels/PreviewViewModel.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/ViewModels/PreviewViewModel.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..ccd1a15
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/ViewModels/PreviewViewModel.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,49 @@
+import Foundation
+import Combine
+
+@MainActor
+class PreviewViewModel: ObservableObject {
+    let fileURL: URL
+    @Published var markdownContent: String = ""
+    @Published var errorMessage: String? = nil
+    @Published var scrollPosition: CGFloat = 0
+
+    private var fileWatcher: FileWatcher?
+
+    init(fileURL: URL) {
+        self.fileURL = fileURL
+        loadFile()
+    }
+
+    func startWatching() {
+        fileWatcher = FileWatcher(url: fileURL) { [weak self] event in
+            Task { @MainActor in
+                self?.handleFileEvent(event)
+            }
+        }
+        fileWatcher?.start()
+    }
+
+    func stopWatching() {
+        fileWatcher?.stop()
+        fileWatcher = nil
+    }
+
+    func loadFile() {
+        do {
+            markdownContent = try String(contentsOf: fileURL, encoding: .utf8)
+            errorMessage = nil
+        } catch {
+            errorMessage = "ファイルを読み込めません: \(error.localizedDescription)"
+        }
+    }
+
+    private func handleFileEvent(_ event: FileWatcher.Event) {
+        switch event {
+        case .modified:
+            loadFile()
+        case .deleted:
+            errorMessage = "ファイルが見つかりません: \(fileURL.lastPathComponent)"
+        }
+    }
+}
diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/MarkdownWebView.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/MarkdownWebView.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..575029c
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/MarkdownWebView.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,132 @@
+import SwiftUI
+import WebKit
+
+struct MarkdownWebView: NSViewRepresentable {
+    let markdownContent: String
+    let baseURL: URL
+    @Binding var scrollPosition: CGFloat
+
+    func makeNSView(context: Context) -> WKWebView {
+        let config = WKWebViewConfiguration()
+
+        let userController = WKUserContentController()
+        userController.add(context.coordinator, name: "scrollPosition")
+        userController.add(context.coordinator, name: "linkClicked")
+        config.userContentController = userController
+
+        let webView = WKWebView(frame: .zero, configuration: config)
+        webView.navigationDelegate = context.coordinator
+        webView.setValue(false, forKey: "drawsBackground")
+
+        let html = HTMLTemplate.build(
+            markdownContent: markdownContent,
+            markedJS: ResourceLoader.loadMarkedJS(),
+            highlightJS: ResourceLoader.loadHighlightJS(),
+            css: ResourceLoader.loadCSS()
+        )
+        webView.loadHTMLString(html, baseURL: baseURL)
+
+        context.coordinator.lastContent = markdownContent
+
+        return webView
+    }
+
+    func updateNSView(_ webView: WKWebView, context: Context) {
+        guard markdownContent != context.coordinator.lastContent else {
+            return
+        }
+        context.coordinator.lastContent = markdownContent
+
+        let escaped = markdownContent
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "\\", with: "\\\\")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "`", with: "\\`")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "$", with: "\\$")
+            .replacingOccurrences(of: "</script>", with: "<\\/script>")
+
+        let js = "updateContent(`\(escaped)`);"
+        webView.evaluateJavaScript(js)
+    }
+
+    func makeCoordinator() -> Coordinator {
+        Coordinator(self)
+    }
+
+    class Coordinator: NSObject, WKNavigationDelegate, WKScriptMessageHandler {
+        let parent: MarkdownWebView
+        var lastContent: String = ""
+
+        init(_ parent: MarkdownWebView) {
+            self.parent = parent
+        }
+
+        // MARK: - WKNavigationDelegate
+
+        func webView(
+            _ webView: WKWebView,
+            decidePolicyFor navigationAction: WKNavigationAction,
+            decisionHandler: @escaping @MainActor @Sendable (WKNavigationActionPolicy) -> Void
+        ) {
+            guard let url = navigationAction.request.url else {
+                decisionHandler(.allow)
+                return
+            }
+
+            // Block javascript: scheme unconditionally
+            if url.scheme == "javascript" {
+                decisionHandler(.cancel)
+                return
+            }
+
+            // Only allow non-link-activated navigations (initial load, etc.)
+            guard navigationAction.navigationType == .linkActivated else {
+                decisionHandler(.allow)
+                return
+            }
+
+            // External http/https links → open in system browser
+            if url.scheme == "http" || url.scheme == "https" {
+                NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
+                decisionHandler(.cancel)
+                return
+            }
+
+            // file: links (relative .md links resolved by baseURL)
+            // Open .md files as new preview windows; open other files in Finder
+            if url.scheme == "file" {
+                if FileValidation.isMarkdownFile(url) {
+                    // Post to linkClicked handler to open as new preview window
+                    // (WindowManager will handle this via the message handler)
+                }
+                // For non-markdown file: links, open in Finder
+                NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
+                decisionHandler(.cancel)
+                return
+            }
+
+            // Block all other link-activated navigations
+            decisionHandler(.cancel)
+        }
+
+        // MARK: - WKScriptMessageHandler
+
+        func userContentController(
+            _ userContentController: WKUserContentController,
+            didReceive message: WKScriptMessage
+        ) {
+            switch message.name {
+            case "scrollPosition":
+                if let position = message.body as? Double {
+                    parent.scrollPosition = CGFloat(position)
+                }
+            case "linkClicked":
+                if let urlString = message.body as? String,
+                   let url = URL(string: urlString),
+                   url.scheme != "javascript" {
+                    NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
+                }
+            default:
+                break
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}
diff --git a/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/PreviewView.swift b/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/PreviewView.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..20e1dcf
--- /dev/null
+++ b/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/PreviewView.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,55 @@
+import SwiftUI
+import UniformTypeIdentifiers
+
+struct PreviewView: View {
+    let fileURL: URL
+    @ObservedObject var windowManager: WindowManager
+    @StateObject private var viewModel: PreviewViewModel
+
+    init(fileURL: URL, windowManager: WindowManager) {
+        self.fileURL = fileURL
+        self.windowManager = windowManager
+        _viewModel = StateObject(wrappedValue: PreviewViewModel(fileURL: fileURL))
+    }
+
+    var body: some View {
+        Group {
+            if let error = viewModel.errorMessage {
+                ErrorView(message: error)
+            } else {
+                MarkdownWebView(
+                    markdownContent: viewModel.markdownContent,
+                    baseURL: fileURL.deletingLastPathComponent(),
+                    scrollPosition: $viewModel.scrollPosition
+                )
+            }
+        }
+        .navigationTitle(fileURL.lastPathComponent)
+        .background(WindowAccessor(url: fileURL.standardizedFileURL))
+        .onAppear {
+            viewModel.startWatching()
+        }
+        .onDisappear {
+            viewModel.stopWatching()
+            windowManager.closeFile(fileURL)
+        }
+        .onDrop(of: [.fileURL], isTargeted: nil) { providers in
+            handleDrop(providers)
+        }
+    }
+
+    private func handleDrop(_ providers: [NSItemProvider]) -> Bool {
+        let hasFileURL = providers.contains { $0.canLoadObject(ofClass: URL.self) }
+        guard hasFileURL else { return false }
+
+        for provider in providers {
+            _ = provider.loadObject(ofClass: URL.self) { url, _ in
+                guard let url, FileValidation.isMarkdownFile(url) else { return }
+                Task { @MainActor in
+                    windowManager.openFile(url)
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        return true
+    }
+}

-# stillmd
-Minimal macOS Markdown previewer
+# StillMD (MarkdownPreviewer)
+
+A lightweight, preview-only Markdown viewer for macOS.
+
+## System Requirements
+
+- macOS 15.5+
+- Xcode 16+
+
+## Build
+
+```bash
+swift build
+```
+
+Or open the project in Xcode and build with ⌘B.
+
+## Usage
+
+- Open `.md` files via File > Open or ⌘O
+- Drag & drop `.md` files onto the window or Dock icon
+- Set as default app for `.md` files in Finder (Get Info > Open With)
+- Auto-reloads when the file is saved externally
+- Follows system light/dark mode
+
+## Features
+
+- GitHub Flavored Markdown (tables, task lists, strikethrough, autolinks)
+- Syntax highlighting for fenced code blocks
+- Relative path resolution for images and links
+- Scroll position preservation on reload
+- One window per file with duplicate detection
+
+## Tech Stack
+
+- SwiftUI + WKWebView
+- [marked.js](https://github.com/markedjs/marked) — Markdown → HTML
+- [highlight.js](https://highlightjs.org/) — syntax highlighting
+
+## License
+
+MIT

./.tmp_review/codex-review-20260404-153305.out.txt:6:  When the app starts without an already-open document, this scene never stores `@Environment(\.openWindow)` into `WindowManager`, because `OpenWindowInjector` is defined but never used here.      1	import SwiftUI
     2	import UniformTypeIdentifiers
     3	
     4	@MainActor
     5	class WindowManager: ObservableObject {
     6	    /// Currently open file URLs (for duplicate detection).
     7	    @Published private(set) var openFiles: Set<URL> = []
     8	
     9	    /// Stored reference to the openWindow action, set by the App entry point
    10	    /// via `OpenWindowInjector` before any file can be opened.
    11	    var openWindowAction: OpenWindowAction?
    12	
    13	    /// Test-only hook: called instead of `openWindowAction` when set.
    14	    /// Allows unit tests to exercise openFile() without a real SwiftUI environment.
    15	    var _testOpenWindowHandler: ((URL) -> Void)?
    16	
    17	    func openFile(_ url: URL) {
    18	        let resolved = url.standardizedFileURL
    19	        if openFiles.contains(resolved) {
    20	            bringToFront(resolved)
    21	            return
    22	        }
    23	
    24	        // In tests, use the test handler; in production, use the real action.
    25	        if let testHandler = _testOpenWindowHandler {
    26	            testHandler(resolved)
    27	        } else {
    28	            guard let action = openWindowAction else { return }
    29	            action(value: resolved)
    30	        }
    31	        openFiles.insert(resolved)
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    func closeFile(_ url: URL) {
    35	        openFiles.remove(url.standardizedFileURL)
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    func showOpenPanel() {
    39	        let panel = NSOpenPanel()
    40	        panel.allowedContentTypes = [
    41	            UTType(filenameExtension: "md")!,
    42	            UTType(filenameExtension: "markdown")!,
    43	        ]
    44	        panel.allowsMultipleSelection = true
    45	        panel.canChooseDirectories = false
    46	        if panel.runModal() == .OK {
    47	            for url in panel.urls {
    48	                openFile(url)
    49	            }
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    private func bringToFront(_ url: URL) {
    54	        for window in NSApp.windows {
    55	            // Match by representedURL (full file URL) for accurate identification
    56	            // when multiple files share the same basename.
    57	            if window.representedURL == url {
    58	                window.makeKeyAndOrderFront(nil)
    59	                return
    60	            }
    61	        }
    62	    }
    63	}

     1	import SwiftUI
     2	import WebKit
     3	
     4	struct MarkdownWebView: NSViewRepresentable {
     5	    let markdownContent: String
     6	    let baseURL: URL
     7	    @Binding var scrollPosition: CGFloat
     8	
     9	    func makeNSView(context: Context) -> WKWebView {
    10	        let config = WKWebViewConfiguration()
    11	
    12	        let userController = WKUserContentController()
    13	        userController.add(context.coordinator, name: "scrollPosition")
    14	        userController.add(context.coordinator, name: "linkClicked")
    15	        config.userContentController = userController
    16	
    17	        let webView = WKWebView(frame: .zero, configuration: config)
    18	        webView.navigationDelegate = context.coordinator
    19	        webView.setValue(false, forKey: "drawsBackground")
    20	
    21	        let html = HTMLTemplate.build(
    22	            markdownContent: markdownContent,
    23	            markedJS: ResourceLoader.loadMarkedJS(),
    24	            highlightJS: ResourceLoader.loadHighlightJS(),
    25	            css: ResourceLoader.loadCSS()
    26	        )
    27	        webView.loadHTMLString(html, baseURL: baseURL)
    28	
    29	        context.coordinator.lastContent = markdownContent
    30	
    31	        return webView
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    func updateNSView(_ webView: WKWebView, context: Context) {
    35	        guard markdownContent != context.coordinator.lastContent else {
    36	            return
    37	        }
    38	        context.coordinator.lastContent = markdownContent
    39	
    40	        let escaped = markdownContent
    41	            .replacingOccurrences(of: "\\", with: "\\\\")
    42	            .replacingOccurrences(of: "`", with: "\\`")
    43	            .replacingOccurrences(of: "$", with: "\\$")
    44	            .replacingOccurrences(of: "</script>", with: "<\\/script>")
    45	
    46	        let js = "updateContent(`\(escaped)`);"
    47	        webView.evaluateJavaScript(js)
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    func makeCoordinator() -> Coordinator {
    51	        Coordinator(self)
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    class Coordinator: NSObject, WKNavigationDelegate, WKScriptMessageHandler {
    55	        let parent: MarkdownWebView
    56	        var lastContent: String = ""
    57	
    58	        init(_ parent: MarkdownWebView) {
    59	            self.parent = parent
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        // MARK: - WKNavigationDelegate
    63	
    64	        func webView(
    65	            _ webView: WKWebView,
    66	            decidePolicyFor navigationAction: WKNavigationAction,
    67	            decisionHandler: @escaping @MainActor @Sendable (WKNavigationActionPolicy) -> Void
    68	        ) {
    69	            guard let url = navigationAction.request.url else {
    70	                decisionHandler(.allow)
    71	                return
    72	            }
    73	
    74	            // Block javascript: scheme unconditionally
    75	            if url.scheme == "javascript" {
    76	                decisionHandler(.cancel)
    77	                return
    78	            }
    79	
    80	            // Only allow non-link-activated navigations (initial load, etc.)
    81	            guard navigationAction.navigationType == .linkActivated else {
    82	                decisionHandler(.allow)
    83	                return
    84	            }
    85	
    86	            // External http/https links → open in system browser
    87	            if url.scheme == "http" || url.scheme == "https" {
    88	                NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
    89	                decisionHandler(.cancel)
    90	                return
    91	            }
    92	
    93	            // file: links (relative .md links resolved by baseURL)
    94	            // Open .md files as new preview windows; open other files in Finder
    95	            if url.scheme == "file" {
    96	                if FileValidation.isMarkdownFile(url) {
    97	                    // Post to linkClicked handler to open as new preview window
    98	                    // (WindowManager will handle this via the message handler)
    99	                }
   100	                // For non-markdown file: links, open in Finder
   101	                NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
   102	                decisionHandler(.cancel)
   103	                return
   104	            }
   105	
   106	            // Block all other link-activated navigations
   107	            decisionHandler(.cancel)
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        // MARK: - WKScriptMessageHandler
   111	
   112	        func userContentController(
   113	            _ userContentController: WKUserContentController,
   114	            didReceive message: WKScriptMessage
   115	        ) {
   116	            switch message.name {
   117	            case "scrollPosition":
   118	                if let position = message.body as? Double {
   119	                    parent.scrollPosition = CGFloat(position)
   120	                }
   121	            case "linkClicked":
   122	                if let urlString = message.body as? String,
   123	                   let url = URL(string: urlString),
   124	                   url.scheme != "javascript" {
   125	                    NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)
   126	                }
   127	            default:
   128	                break
   129	            }
   130	        }
   131	    }
   132	}

/bin/zsh -lc "sed -n '1,220p' .tmp_review/codex-review-20260404-153305.out.txt && echo '---ERR---' && sed -n '1,260p' .tmp_review/codex-review-20260404-153305.err.txt" in /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd
 succeeded in 0ms:
The new previewer has multiple functional regressions in core workflows: opening files from inside the app is currently broken, local Markdown links are inert, syntax highlighting is not actually visible, and file watching can stop permanently after slower delete/recreate saves. Those issues mean the patch is not ready to be considered correct.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Inject the openWindow action before calling openFile — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/App/MarkdownPreviewerApp.swift:8-10
  When the app starts without an already-open document, this scene never stores `@Environment(\.openWindow)` into `WindowManager`, because `OpenWindowInjector` is defined but never used here. In that state `WindowManager.openFile` hits `guard let action = openWindowAction else { return }`, so File > Open and drag-dropping another file from an existing window both become no-ops unless the app was launched by an external document event.

- [P2] Open relative file links instead of cancelling them — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/MarkdownWebView.swift:93-97
  Any Markdown link that resolves to a local `file:` URL is cancelled here, while the JS click handler only forwards `http/https`, so links like `[other](other.md)` or `[image](./notes/readme.md)` are dead. Because `loadHTMLString` already uses the document directory as `baseURL`, this breaks the advertised relative-link support for local Markdown cross-links.

- [P2] Add highlight.js token styles to the bundled CSS — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/Resources/preview.css:92-105
  These rules style the code block container, but the bundle never defines any `.hljs` / `.hljs-*` selectors. `hljs.highlightAll()` will still wrap tokens in span classes, yet without a theme those spans inherit the normal code color, so fenced code blocks remain visually monochrome in both light and dark mode despite claiming syntax highlighting support.

- [P2] Restart the watcher after slow delete/recreate saves — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/FileWatcher.swift:79-87
  If an editor saves by renaming the file away and recreating it more than 200ms later, this branch only emits `.deleted` and keeps the dispatch source attached to the old vnode. After that, recreating the file at the same path produces no further events, so auto-reload stays broken until the user closes and reopens the preview.

    60	    private func handleWrite() {
    61	        readWithRetry(attempt: 0)

    64	    private func readWithRetry(attempt: Int) {
    65	        if FileManager.default.isReadableFile(atPath: url.path) {
    66	            callback(.modified)
    67	        } else if attempt < maxRetries {
    68	            DispatchQueue.global().asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + retryDelay) {
    69	                self.readWithRetry(attempt: attempt + 1)
    70	            }
    71	        } else {
    72	            callback(.deleted)
    73	        }
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    private func handleDeleteOrRename() {
    77	        // Editors often save by renaming the file away and recreating it.
    78	        // Wait briefly then re-check existence. Use multiple retries for
    79	        // slower save operations.
    80	        retryRestart(attempt: 0, maxAttempts: 5, delay: 0.2)
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    private func retryRestart(attempt: Int, maxAttempts: Int, delay: TimeInterval) {
    84	        DispatchQueue.global().asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + delay) { [weak self] in
    85	            guard let self else { return }
    86	            if FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: self.url.path) {
    87	                // File was re-created — restart monitoring
    88	                self.stop()
    89	                self.start()
    90	                self.callback(.modified)
    91	            } else if attempt < maxAttempts {
    92	                // File not yet recreated — retry with increasing delay
    93	                self.retryRestart(attempt: attempt + 1, maxAttempts: maxAttempts, delay: delay)
    94	            } else {
    95	                self.callback(.deleted)
    96	            }
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    deinit {
   101	        stop()
   102	    }
   103	}

codex
The patch introduces a core regression where in-app open workflows never work because `openWindowAction` is never initialized. It also has additional functional gaps around local Markdown link handling and watcher recovery, so the change is not correct as submitted.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Mount the `openWindow` injector before using `WindowManager` — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/App/MarkdownPreviewerApp.swift:8-13
  `WindowManager.openFile(_:)` can only open a new preview if `openWindowAction` has been filled from the SwiftUI environment, but this scene never mounts `OpenWindowInjector` anywhere. In production that means `openWindowAction` stays `nil` for the entire app lifetime, so both File ▸ Open and dropping another Markdown file onto an existing window silently do nothing.

- [P2] Open local Markdown links inside the previewer instead of via LaunchServices — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/Views/MarkdownWebView.swift:95-102
  This `file:` branch always falls through to `NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)`, even when the target is another Markdown document. As a result, clicking `[other.md](other.md)` only works if StillMD is already the system default handler for `.md`; otherwise the link opens in some other app, which breaks in-app cross-document navigation despite the comment above promising a new preview window.

- [P2] Keep watching after a delayed delete/recreate save — /Users/justinwulf/Documents/justin/work/querylift/service/stillmd/MarkdownPreviewer/Services/FileWatcher.swift:83-95
  Once these retries are exhausted, the watcher only emits `.deleted` and never reattaches to the path. Because the dispatch source is still bound to the old vnode, any editor or generator that recreates the file more than ~1.2s later leaves auto-reload permanently broken until the user closes and reopens the preview.
